[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This type of vulnerability occurs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen an application executes operating system commands using data that can be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrolled or influenced by an attacker, potentially allowing arbitrary command [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution on the host system.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Satisfies fuzzer:** The OsCommandInjection sanitizer will no longer detect [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe vulnerability[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Security best practice:** Follows principle of least privilege - compression[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries should only compress/decompress, not execute commands[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Expected Outcomes[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**After applying this fix:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security:** The OS Command Injection vulnerability is completely eliminated[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Functionality:** All legitimate GZIP decompression operations work identically[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Testing:** All existing unit tests pass without modification[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzing:** The fuzzer no longer detects the vulnerability[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Metadata:** File names and all other GZIP header metadata remain accessible[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Compatibility:** No breaking changes to the public API[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Validation steps:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Run the fuzzer again with the same test case - should not trigger security [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Execute all existing unit tests - should pass without changes[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify filename metadata is still accessible via `[0m[1;35mgetMetaData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Confirm no ProcessBuilder usage in GzipCompressorInputStream outside of test [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side effects:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected. The removed code had no legitimate purpose.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Risk mitigation:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The removed code only executed when `modTime == 1731695077L` AND `fname != null`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This specific condition was never part of legitimate functionality[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No existing tests depend on this behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit's malicious[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- File name metadata is still stored and accessible [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m396[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Evidence from other compressor implementations:**[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReviewing the codebase structure:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `XzCompressorInputStream` - No ProcessBuilder usage[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `BrotliCompressorInputStream` - No ProcessBuilder usage  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `SnappyCompressorInputStream` - No ProcessBuilder usage[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `Pack200CompressorInputStream` - No ProcessBuilder usage[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `GzipCompressorOutputStream` - Writes filenames as metadata, never executes them[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe only ProcessBuilder usage in the codebase is in test utilities [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSparseFilesTest.java, ZipFileTest.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for legitimate test setup, not production [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis confirms that **removing the ProcessBuilder call from [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGzipCompressorInputStream is the correct fix** to align with the rest of the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase architecture.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
